""SELECT t.\"Id\", t.\"Id0\", (\"x.Flight\".\"CarrierCode\" || \"x.Flight\".\"FlightNumber\") AS \"FlightNumber\", \"x.Flight\".\"DepartureAirport\", \"x.Flight\".\"ArrivalAirport\", CAST(\"x.Flight\".\"DepartureDate\" AS text) AS \"DepartureDate\", CAST(\"x.Flight\".\"ArrivalDate\" AS text) AS \"ArrivalDate\", \"x.Booking.BookingFlight\".\"BookingId\"
